  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                     <div class="wrap"> 
                      <strong title="Bug behavior facts" class="name">Bug behavior facts:</strong> 
                      <div id="customfield_12310200-val" class="value type-multicheckboxes" data-fieldtype="multicheckboxes" data-fieldtypecompletekey="com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.customfieldtypes:multicheckboxes">

              <div id="descriptionmodule" class="module toggle-wrap">
               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>I got a report of the following intermittent (6/60) exception in store.RecoveryAfterBackupTest.<br> Exception in thread "main" java.security.AccessControlException: Access denied ("java.lang.RuntimePermission" "modifyThread")<br> at java.security.AccessController.throwACE(AccessController.java:100)<br> at java.security.AccessController.checkPermission(AccessController.java:174)<br> at java.lang.SecurityManager.checkPermission(SecurityManager.java:549)<br> at java.lang.SecurityManager.checkAccess(SecurityManager.java:676)<br> at java.lang.Thread.checkAccess(Thread.java:459)<br> at java.lang.Thread.interrupt(Thread.java:588)<br> at org.apache.derby.iapi.services.context.ContextService$1.run(Unknown Source)<br> at java.security.AccessController.doPrivileged(AccessController.java:274)<br> at org.apache.derby.iapi.services.context.ContextService.notifyAllActiveThreads(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.impl.services.monitor.BaseMonitor.shutdown(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.jdbc.InternalDriver.connect(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.jdbc.Driver20.connect(Unknown Source)<br> at org.apache.derby.jdbc.AutoloadedDriver.connect(Unknown Source)<br> at java.sql.DriverManager.getConnection(DriverManager.java:571)<br> at java.sql.DriverManager.getConnection(DriverManager.java:233)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.functionTests.util.TestUtil.getConnection(TestUtil.java:836)<br> at org.apache.derbyTesting.functionTests.tests.store.RecoveryAfterBackup.main(RecoveryAfterBackup.java:82)</p> 
                  <p>modifyThread is a necessary permission if interrupting a thread other than the current thread but is not in our policy file for derby.jar.</p> 
                  <p>The relevant code in ContextService is:<br> for (ContextManager cm : allContexts) {</p> 
                  <p> Thread active = cm.activeThread;</p> 
                  <p> if (active == me)<br> continue;</p> 
                  <p> if (active == null)<br> continue;</p> 
                  <p> final Thread fActive = active;<br> if (cm.setInterrupted(c))<br> {<br> AccessController.doPrivileged(<br> new PrivilegedAction&lt;Void&gt;() {<br> public Void run() </p> { fActive.interrupt(); return null; } 
                  <p> });<br> }</p> 
                  <p>I am not sure why this has never come up before. Are we expecting in this context that fActive is the current thread?</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>
